## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Bazel Starlark Evaluation and BUILD File Migration Inventory

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in bazelbuild/bazel under src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/packages/ and src/main/java/net/starlark/ that implement Starlark evaluation for BUILD files. Identify: the StarlarkThread class and its environment setup, the PackageFactory that invokes Starlark evaluation, the BzlLoadFunction for .bzl file loading, the rule() and macro() builtin function implementations, and the Package.Builder that accumulates targets. Report each file path and key class.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/bazel--8.0.0.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

Perfect! I've successfully created a comprehensive inventory of the Java source files implementing Starlark evaluation for BUILD files in Bazel 8.0.0. 

## Summary

I've identified and documented **11 key Java files and classes** that form the Starlark evaluation architecture:

### Core Components:
1. **StarlarkThread** - The execution context for Starlark code evaluation
2. **PackageFactory** - Orchestrates BUILD file evaluation and package construction
3. **BzlLoadFunction** - Handles .bzl file loading within the dependency graph
4. **Package.Builder** - Accumulates targets during BUILD file evaluation
5. **StarlarkRuleClassFunctions** - Implements rule() and macro() builtins
6. **StarlarkRuleFunction** - Represents callable rule definitions
7. **MacroFunction** - Represents callable macro definitions
8. **RuleFactory** - Provides native rule implementations
9. **StarlarkGlobals** - Defines environment symbols
10. **BazelStarlarkEnvironment** - Manages complete Starlark environment

The output has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed information about each file path, symbol names, the evaluation chain, and a comprehensive narrative explaining how these components work together to evaluate BUILD files through Starlark.

Files\\n\\nThe Bazel codebase implements Starlark evaluation for BUILD files through a coordinated system of key components:\\n\\n### 1. StarlarkThread (src/main/java/net/starlark/java/eval/StarlarkThread.java)\\n**Class: StarlarkThread** (line 47)\\nThis is the core execution context for Starlark code. It maintains the evaluation state, call stack, and environment for executing Starlark statements. The StarlarkThread is created with a Mutability scope and carries StarlarkSemantics that control language-level feature flags. It provides environment setup through thread-local storage and manages the execution lifecycle of Starlark programs, including BUILD files.\\n\\n### 2. PackageFactory (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/packages/PackageFactory.java)\\n**Class: PackageFactory** (line 80)\\nResponsible for constructing Package instances from BUILD files. It orchestrates the Starlark evaluation by invoking the interpreter with the appropriate environment. The PackageFactory holds the RuleClassProvider, which supplies the available rule definitions, and coordinates the overall package loading process. It prepares the execution environment and manages the interaction between the Starlark interpreter and Bazel's package model.\\n\\n### 3. BzlLoadFunction (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/skyframe/BzlLoadFunction.java)\\n**Class: BzlLoadFunction** (line 108)\\nImplements SkyFunction to handle the loading and evaluation of .bzl files within the Skyframe dependency graph. BzlLoadFunction manages the loading of Starlark modules (*.bzl files), handles exports, and maintains the cache of compiled .bzl files. It establishes the Starlark environment for .bzl evaluation, including the registration of functions like rule() and macro() before delegating to the Starlark interpreter.\\n\\n### 4. Package.Builder (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/packages/Package.java)\\n**Class: Package.Builder** (line 1059)\\nExtends TargetDefinitionContext and accumulates targets during BUILD file evaluation. The Builder pattern implementation maintains the mutable state while the Package itself is immutable. It collects rules, file targets, and macros as they are declared during Starlark evaluation. The Builder tracks target names, prevents conflicts, manages macro namespaces, and ultimately constructs the immutable Package object upon completion.\\n\\n### 5. rule() Builtin Function (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/analysis/starlark/StarlarkRuleClassFunctions.java)\\n**Method: rule()** (line 493) in class **StarlarkRuleClassFunctions**\\nImplements the builtin rule() function that creates Starlark-defined rule types. It accepts a StarlarkFunction implementation, attribute definitions, and rule metadata (test flag, executable flag, etc.). The method validates parameters, constructs a RuleClass.Builder, processes attributes, and returns a StarlarkRuleFunction callable that can instantiate rule instances in BUILD files.\\n\\n### 6. StarlarkRuleFunction (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/analysis/starlark/StarlarkRuleClassFunctions.java)\\n**Class: StarlarkRuleFunction** (line 1567) in **StarlarkRuleClassFunctions**\\nRepresents the return value of rule() - a callable Starlark value that instantiates rule objects. It implements StarlarkExportable (for exporting from .bzl files) and RuleFunction interfaces. When invoked during BUILD file evaluation, it creates Rule instances and adds them to the package via Package.Builder.\\n\\n### 7. macro() Builtin Function (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/analysis/starlark/StarlarkRuleClassFunctions.java)\\n**Method: macro()** (line 362) in class **StarlarkRuleClassFunctions**\\nImplements the builtin macro() function for creating symbolic macros. It accepts a StarlarkFunction implementation, attribute dictionary, inheritance specifications, and finalization flags. MacroFunction (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/analysis/starlark/StarlarkRuleClassFunctions.java)\\n**Class: MacroFunction** (line 1392) in **StarlarkRuleClassFunctions**\\nRepresents a symbolic macro - the return value of macro(). When invoked in a BUILD file, it expands the macro's implementation function in a separate Starlark evaluation context, typically creating multiple targets under a namespace derived from the macro's name parameter.\\n\\n### 9. RuleFactory (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/packages/RuleFactory.java)\\n**Class: BuiltinRuleFunction** (line 289) in **RuleFactory**\\nImplements rule instantiation for native (built-in) rules. BuiltinRuleFunction is a StarlarkCallable wrapper around native RuleClass objects, allowing them to be invoked from BUILD files and Starlark code. StarlarkGlobals Interface (src/main/java/com/google/devtools/build/lib/packages/StarlarkGlobals.java)\\n**Interface: StarlarkGlobals** (line 33)\\nDefines the standard environment symbols available in different Starlark contexts (BUILD files, .bzl files, etc.). It provides methods like getFixedBuildFileToplevels() and getFixedBzlToplevels() that return the predeclared symbols and their values.\\n\\n### 11.
